
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Diagnosis - Count - Difference from Same Period Previous Year - By - Fiscal Date - Diagnosis - Start]
AS [Measures].[Diagnosis - Count] - (PARALLELPERIOD([Date - Diagnosis - Start].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].[Fiscal Year], 1, [Date - Diagnosis - Start].[Fiscal Year].CurrentMember) , ([Measures].[Diagnosis - Count]))
,VISIBLE=1, DISPLAY_FOLDER='Difference\Difference by Fiscal Year', FORMAT_STRING='#,##0;-#,##0', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='Diagnosis';

CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Diagnosis - Count - Growth from Same Period Previous Year - By - Fiscal Date - Diagnosis - Start]
 AS IIF ((PARALLELPERIOD([Date - Diagnosis - Start].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].[Fiscal Year], 1, [Date - Diagnosis - Start].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].CurrentMember) , ([Measures].[Diagnosis - Count])) = 0  , NULL,
    IIF ([Measures].[Diagnosis - Count] = 0, NULL,
            (
            [Measures].[Diagnosis - Count] - 
            (PARALLELPERIOD([Date - Diagnosis - Start].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].[Fiscal Year], 1, [Date - Diagnosis - Start].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].CurrentMember) , ([Measures].[Diagnosis - Count])
                            )
            )
            / (PARALLELPERIOD([Date - Diagnosis - Start].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].[Fiscal Year], 1, [Date - Diagnosis - Start].[Fiscal Year - Quarter - Month - Date].CurrentMember) , ([Measures].[Diagnosis - Count])
            )
        )
) 
,VISIBLE=1, DISPLAY_FOLDER='Growth\Growth by Fiscal Year', FORMAT_STRING='Percent', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='Diagnosis';

create member CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Diagnosis - Count - Percent Rank Excluding Null All] as
IIF(count((Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, [Measures].[Diagnosis - Count])) <= 1
	or Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER is Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER
	or Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER is Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER,
	NULL,
	1.0 - (
		RANK(
			Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER, 
			except(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, { Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER, Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER }), 
			[Measures].[Diagnosis - Count]
		) - 1.0
	) / (
		count(
			(
				except(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, { Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER, Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER }),
				[Measures].[Diagnosis - Count]
			)
		) - 1.0
	)
)
,VISIBLE=1, DISPLAY_FOLDER='Rank\Percent Rank Excluding Null All', FORMAT_STRING='Percent', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='Diagnosis';

create member CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Diagnosis - Count - Percent Rank Including Null All] as
IIF((count((Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, [Measures].[Diagnosis - Count])) - 1.0) <= 1,
	NULL,
	1.0 - (
		RANK(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER, 
			Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, 
			[Measures].[Diagnosis - Count]
		) -1.0
	) / (count((Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, [Measures].[Diagnosis - Count])) - 1.0)
)
,VISIBLE=1, DISPLAY_FOLDER='Rank\Percent Rank Including Null All', FORMAT_STRING='Percent', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='Diagnosis';

CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Diagnosis - Count - Percentage Of Total]
 AS 
IIF(([Measures].[Diagnosis - Count], Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CurrentMember.Parent) = 0, 
     null,
     [Measures].[Diagnosis - Count]/([Measures].[Diagnosis - Count], Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CurrentMember.Parent)
    )
,VISIBLE=1, DISPLAY_FOLDER='Percentage Of Total', FORMAT_STRING='Percent', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='Diagnosis';

	or Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER is Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER

	NULL,

		RANK(
			Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER, 
			except(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, { Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER, Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER }), 
			[Measures].[ED Visit - Advance Directive Printed to ED Discharge in Minutes - Arithmetic Average]
		) - 1.0
	) / (
		count(
			(
				except(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, { Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER, Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER }),

			)
		) - 1.0

,VISIBLE=1, DISPLAY_FOLDER='Rank\Percent Rank Excluding Null All', FORMAT_STRING='Percent', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='ED Visit';

IIF(([Measures].[ED Visit - Lab Completed to Provider Reviewed in Minutes Log - Sum], Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CurrentMember.Parent) = 0, 
     null,
     [Measures].[ED Visit - Lab Completed to Provider Reviewed in Minutes Log - Sum]/([Measures].[ED Visit - Lab Completed to Provider Reviewed in Minutes Log - Sum], Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CurrentMember.Parent)
    )
,VISIBLE=1, DISPLAY_FOLDER='Percentage Of Total', FORMAT_STRING='Percent', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='ED Visit';

create member CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[ED Visit - Lab Ordered to Lab Completed in Miinutes - Count - Percent Rank Excluding Null All] as
IIF(count((Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, [Measures].[ED Visit - Lab Ordered to Lab Completed in Miinutes - Count])) <= 1
	or Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER is Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER
	or Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER is Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER,
	NULL,
	1.0 - (
		RANK(
			Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER, 
			except(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, { Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER, Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER }), 
			[Measures].[ED Visit - Lab Ordered to Lab Completed in Miinutes - Count]
		) - 1.0
	) / (
		count(
			(
				except(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, { Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER, Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER }),
				[Measures].[ED Visit - Lab Ordered to Lab Completed in Miinutes - Count]
			)
		) - 1.0
	)
)
,VISIBLE=1, DISPLAY_FOLDER='Rank\Percent Rank Excluding Null All', FORMAT_STRING='Percent', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='ED Visit';

create member CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[ED Visit - Lab Ordered to Lab Completed in Miinutes - Count - Percent Rank Including Null All] as
IIF((count((Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, [Measures].[ED Visit - Lab Ordered to Lab Completed in Miinutes - Count])) - 1.0) <= 1,
	NULL,
	1.0 - (
		RANK(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER, 
			Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, 
			[Measures].[ED Visit - Lab Ordered to Lab Completed in Miinutes - Count]
		) -1.0
	) / (count((Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, [Measures].[ED Visit - Lab Ordered to Lab Completed in Miinutes - Count])) - 1.0)
)
,VISIBLE=1, DISPLAY_FOLDER='Rank\Percent Rank Including Null All', FORMAT_STRING='Percent', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='ED Visit';

IIF(([Measures].[ED Visit - Triage Start to Patient Roomed in Minutes - Geometric Average], Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CurrentMember.Parent) = 0, 
     null,
     [Measures].[ED Visit - Triage Start to Patient Roomed in Minutes - Geometric Average]/([Measures].[ED Visit - Triage Start to Patient Roomed in Minutes - Geometric Average], Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CurrentMember.Parent)
    )
,VISIBLE=1, DISPLAY_FOLDER='Percentage Of Total', FORMAT_STRING='Percent', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='ED Visit';

create member CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[ED Visit - Triage Start to Triage Complete in Minutes - Arithmetic Average - Percent Rank Excluding Null All] as
IIF(count((Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, [Measures].[ED Visit - Triage Start to Triage Complete in Minutes - Arithmetic Average])) <= 1
	or Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER is Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER
	or Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER is Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER,
	NULL,
	1.0 - (
		RANK(
			Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER, 
			except(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, { Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER, Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER }), 
			[Measures].[ED Visit - Triage Start to Triage Complete in Minutes - Arithmetic Average]
		) - 1.0
	) / (
		count(
			(
				except(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, { Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER, Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER }),
				[Measures].[ED Visit - Triage Start to Triage Complete in Minutes - Arithmetic Average]
			)
		) - 1.0
	)
)
,VISIBLE=1, DISPLAY_FOLDER='Rank\Percent Rank Excluding Null All', FORMAT_STRING='Percent', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='ED Visit';

create member CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[ED Visit - Triage Start to Triage Complete in Minutes - Arithmetic Average - Percent Rank Including Null All] as
IIF((count((Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, [Measures].[ED Visit - Triage Start to Triage Complete in Minutes - Arithmetic Average])) - 1.0) <= 1,
	NULL,
